From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The [S&P 500](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%26P_500 "S&P 500") is a [stock market index](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stock_market_index "Stock market index") maintained by [S&P Dow Jones Indices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%26P_Dow_Jones_Indices "S&P Dow Jones Indices"). It comprises 503 [common stocks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Common_stock "Common stock") which are issued by 500 [large-cap](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Market_capitalization "Market capitalization") companies traded on the American stock exchanges (including the 30 companies that compose the [Dow Jones Industrial Average](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average "Dow Jones Industrial Average")). The index includes about 80 percent of the American market by capitalization. It is weighted by [free-float](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capitalization-weighted_index#Free-float_weighting "Capitalization-weighted index") market capitalization, so more valuable companies account for relatively more weight in the index. The index constituents and the constituent weights are updated regularly using rules published by S&P Dow Jones Indices. Although called the S&P 500, the index contains 503 stocks because it includes two share classes of stock from 3 of its component companies.[\[1\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-1)[\[2\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-2)

## Selected changes to the list of S&P 500 components

\[ [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_S%26P_500_companies&action=edit&section=2 "Edit section: Selected changes to the list of S&P 500 components")\]

S&P Dow Jones Indices updates the components of the [S&P 500](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%26P_500_Index "S&P 500 Index") periodically, typically in response to acquisitions, or to keep the index up to date as various companies grow or shrink in value.[\[3\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-3) Between January 1, 1963, and December 31, 2014, 1,186 index components were replaced by other components.

| Ticker | Security | Ticker | Security |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| August 28, 2025 | IBKR | [Interactive Brokers](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interactive_Brokers "Interactive Brokers") | WBA | [Walgreens Boots Alliance](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walgreens_Boots_Alliance "Walgreens Boots Alliance") | Sycamore acquired Walgreen Boots Alliance.[\[4\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-4) |
| July 23, 2025 | XYZ | [Block, Inc.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Block,_Inc. "Block, Inc.") | HES | [Hess Corporation](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hess_Corporation "Hess Corporation") | S&P 500 and S&P 100 constituent Chevron Corp. acquired Hess Corp.[\[5\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-5) |
| July 18, 2025 | TTD | [Trade Desk (The)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Trade_Desk "The Trade Desk") | ANSS | [Ansys](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ansys "Ansys") | S&P 500 constituent Synopsys Inc. acquired Ansys.[\[6\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies#cite_note-6) |
